<script>
function IsPC() {
    var flag = true;
    if(getParam("type")){
    	flag = true;
    }else{
    	var userAgentInfo = navigator.userAgent;
	    var Agents = ["Android", "iPhone",
	                "SymbianOS", "Windows Phone",
	                "iPad", "iPod"];
	    for (var v = 0; v < Agents.length; v++) {
	        if (userAgentInfo.indexOf(Agents[v]) > 0) {
	            flag = false;
	            break;
	        }
	    }
    }
    return flag;
}
var flag = IsPC(); //true为PC端，false为手机端
//console.log(flag);

function getParam(paramName) { 
    paramValue = "", isFound = !1; 
    if (this.location.search.indexOf("?") == 0 && this.location.search.indexOf("=") > 1) { 
        arrSource = decodeURI(this.location.search).substring(1, this.location.search.length).split("&"), i = 0; 
        while (i < arrSource.length && !isFound) arrSource[i].indexOf("=") > 0 && arrSource[i].split("=")[0].toLowerCase() == paramName.toLowerCase() && (paramValue = arrSource[i].split("=")[1], isFound = !0), i++ 
    } 
    return paramValue == "" && (paramValue = null), paramValue 
}

if(!flag){
	window.location.href="/eptemp.aspx?t=Znzw.HMobile.Hindex&istest=1"
}

</script>

//获取用户登录信息保存用户足迹
var saveparam={
	"userid":"",//用户id
	"title":"",//标题
	"keyword":"",//关键词
	"fwurl":"",//页面地址
	"itemcode":"",//事项编码
	"itemname":"",//事项名称
	"itemtype":"",//事项类型
	"typename":"",//类型名称
	"areacode":""//区域编码
}

function getUserInfo($,param){
	$yt.ajax.post("","e:YiTian.action.LoginAction.Get","",function(res){
         		console.log("获取用户登录信息保存用户足迹");
		 		console.log(res);
 		if(res.code=="0"){
 			if(res.data!=null){
 				if(res.data.UserID>0){
 					param.userid=res.data.UserID;
 					saveUserZj($,param);
 				}else{
 					param.userid='';
 					saveUserZj($,param);
 				}
 			}else{
 				param.userid='';
 				saveUserZj($,param);
 			}
 		}else{
 			param.userid='';
 			saveUserZj($,param);
 		}
 	},true,"",true);
}

//保存用户足迹
function saveUserZj($,param){
	/*zinfo//json实体//
	*
	*userid//用户id
	*title//标题
	*keyword//关键词
	*fwurl//页面地址
	*itemcode//事项编码
	*itemname//事项名称
	*itemtype//事项类型
	*typename//类型名称
	*areacode//区域编码
	*
	*/
	console.log(param);
	saveparam.userid=param.userid;
	saveparam.title=param.title.replace(/\s*/g,"");
	saveparam.keyword=param.keyword;
	saveparam.fwurl=param.fwurl;
	saveparam.itemcode=param.itemcode;
	saveparam.itemname=param.itemname.replace(/\s*/g,"");
	saveparam.itemtype=param.itemtype;
	saveparam.typename=param.typename.replace(/\s*/g,"");
	saveparam.areacode=param.areacode;
	$yt.ajax.post("ZWBSDB","e:ZnzwSvr.action.UserZJAction.SaveUserZJ",saveparam,function(res){
		console.log('保存用户足迹');
		console.log(param);
		console.log(res);
		if(res.code=="0"){
			if(res.data==true){
				console.log('保存成功');
			}
		}
	},true,"",true);
}
/** 
 * 获取指定的URL参数值 
 * URL:http://www.quwan.com/index?name=tyler 
 * 参数：paramName URL参数 
 * 调用方法:getParam("name") 
 * 返回值:tyler 
 */ 
function getParam(paramName) {
    paramValue = "", isFound = !1; 
    if (this.location.search.indexOf("?") == 0 && this.location.search.indexOf("=") > 1) { 
        arrSource = decodeURI(this.location.search).substring(1, this.location.search.length).split("&"), i = 0; 
        while (i < arrSource.length && !isFound) arrSource[i].indexOf("=") > 0 && arrSource[i].split("=")[0].toLowerCase() == paramName.toLowerCase() && (paramValue = arrSource[i].split("=")[1], isFound = !0), i++ 
    } 
    if(paramValue==null || paramValue==""){
       return paramValue  == "" && (paramValue  = null), paramValue
    }else{
       return removeXss(paramValue);
    }
    //return paramValue  == "" && (paramValue  = null), paramValue?removeXss(paramValue):null
}

function removeXss(val)
    {
        val = val.replace(/([\x00-\x08][\x0b-\x0c][\x0e-\x20])/g, '');

        var search = 'abcdefghijklmnopqrstuvwxyz';
        search += 'ABCDEFGHIJKLMNOPQRSTUVWXYZ';
        search += '1234567890!@#$%^&*()';
        search += '~`";:?+/={}[]-_|\'\\';

        for (var i = 0; i < search.length; i++) {
            var re = new RegExp('(&#[x|X]0{0,8}'+ parseInt(search[i].charCodeAt(),16)+';?)','gi');
            val = val.replace(re, search[i]);
            re = new RegExp('(&#0{0,8}'+ search[i].charCodeAt() + ';?)','gi');
            val = val.replace(re, search[i]);
        }

        var ra1 = ['javascript', 'vbscript', 'expression', 'applet', 'meta','blink', 'link',  'script', 'embed', 'object', 'iframe', 'frame', 'frameset', 'ilayer', 'layer', 'bgsound', 'title'];
        var ra2 = ['onabort', 'onactivate', 'onafterprint', 'onafterupdate', 'onbeforeactivate', 'onbeforecopy', 'onbeforecut', 'onbeforedeactivate', 'onbeforeeditfocus', 'onbeforepaste', 'onbeforeprint', 'onbeforeunload', 'onbeforeupdate', 'onblur', 'onbounce', 'oncellchange', 'onchange', 'onclick', 'oncontextmenu', 'oncontrolselect', 'oncopy', 'oncut', 'ondataavailable', 'ondatasetchanged', 'ondatasetcomplete', 'ondblclick', 'ondeactivate', 'ondrag', 'ondragend', 'ondragenter', 'ondragleave', 'ondragover', 'ondragstart', 'ondrop', 'onerror', 'onerrorupdate', 'onfilterchange', 'onfinish', 'onfocus', 'onfocusin', 'onfocusout', 'onhelp', 'onkeydown', 'onkeypress', 'onkeyup', 'onlayoutcomplete', 'onload', 'onlosecapture', 'onmousedown', 'onmouseenter', 'onmouseleave', 'onmousemove', 'onmouseout', 'onmouseover', 'onmouseup', 'onmousewheel', 'onmove', 'onmoveend', 'onmovestart', 'onpaste', 'onpropertychange', 'onreadystatechange', 'onreset', 'onresize', 'onresizeend', 'onresizestart', 'onrowenter', 'onrowexit', 'onrowsdelete', 'onrowsinserted', 'onscroll', 'onselect', 'onselectionchange', 'onselectstart', 'onstart', 'onstop', 'onsubmit', 'onunload'];
        var ra = [].concat(ra1, ra2);

        var found = true;
        while (found == true) {
            var val_before = val;
            for (var i = 0; i < ra.length; i++) {
                var pattern = '';
                for (var j = 0; j < ra[i].length; j++) {
                    if (j > 0) {
                        pattern += '(';
                        pattern += '(&#[x|X]0{0,8}([9][a][b]);?)?';
                        pattern += '|(&#0{0,8}([9][10][13]);?)?';
                        pattern += ')?';
                    }
                    pattern += ra[i][j];
                }
                parttern = new RegExp(pattern,'gi');
                var replacement = ra[i].substr(0, 2) + '<x>'+ ra[i].substr(2);
                val = val.replace(parttern, replacement);
                if (val_before  == val) {
                    found = false;
                }
            }
        }
        return val;
  }

function replaceParamVal(paramName,replaceWith) {
    var oUrl = this.location.href.toString();
    var re=eval('/('+ paramName+'=)([^&]*)/gi');
    var nUrl = oUrl.replace(re,paramName+'='+replaceWith);
    console.log(nUrl);
    return nUrl;
}

//修改地址参数
function changeURLArg(url,arg,arg_val){ 
   var pattern=arg+'=([^&]*)'; 
   var replaceText=arg+'='+arg_val; 
   if(url.match(pattern)){ 
       var tmp='/('+ arg+'=)([^&]*)/gi'; 
       tmp=url.replace(eval(tmp),replaceText); 
       return tmp; 
   }else{ 
       if(url.match('[\?]')){ 
           return url+'&'+replaceText; 
       }else{ 
           return url+'?'+replaceText; 
       } 
  } 
   return url+'\n'+arg+'\n'+arg_val; 
}

	parent.layer.open({
	  type: 2,
	  title:title?title:false,
	  shadeClose: false,
	  shade: 0.5,
	  area: ['60%', '80%'],
	  closeBtn:2,
	  scrollbar:false,
	  move:false,
	  content: url //iframe的url
	});
}

//获取智能消息提醒
function znMsg($,atag,content,islogin){
	if(content){
		var i=0;
		var timer;
		if(islogin == true){
			$(".txbox").show();
			$(".txbox").addClass('layui-anim-scale');
			timer = setInterval(function(){
		        $('.wz-div').text(content.substring(0, i));
		        i++;
		        if( $('.wz-div').text()==content){
		            clearInterval(timer);
		        };
		    },200);
		    $yt.play.tts(content,"https://zwfw.guizhou.gov.cn");
		}else if(islogin == false){
			timer = setInterval(function(){
		        $('.ts').text(content.substring(0, i));
		        i++;
		        if( $('.ts').text()==content){
		            clearInterval(timer);
		        };
		    },200);
		    $yt.play.tts(content,"https://zwfw.guizhou.gov.cn");
		}
	}else{
		$yt.ajax.post("","e:ZnzwSvr.action.AlertAction.getAlert",{"atag":atag},function(res){
			console.log("获取智能消息提醒");
		   console.log(res)
		   if(res.code=="0"){
		   	var data=res.data
		   	if(data){
		   		if(data.acontent){
			   		$(".txbox").show();
			   		$(".txbox").addClass('layui-anim-scale');
				   //$yt.play.tts("您好，欢迎来到淘政务主题服务馆，我是客服小姐姐，贵宝","http://103.3.152.215:84");
				   var str=data.acontent;
				   var i=0;
				   var timer = setInterval(function(){
				        $('.wz-div').text(str.substring(0, i));
				        $('.ts').text(str.substring(0, i));
				        i++;
				        if($('.wz-div').text()==str){
				            clearInterval(timer);
				        };
				         if( $('.ts').text()==str){
				            clearInterval(timer);
				        };
				    },200);
			   		$yt.play.tts(data.acontent,"https://zwfw.guizhou.gov.cn");
			   	}
		   	}
		   	var t = setInterval(function(){
				$(".txbox").hide();
				$(".txbox").removeClass('layui-anim-scale');
				 clearInterval(t);
			}, 15000);
		   }
		  },true,"",true);
	  }
}
function navhd(grbsnav,item,spantag){
	// 鼠标放在哪个li上面，span对应一道到哪里，移开后回到原位置
    var grbsnav=document.getElementById(grbsnav);
    var liArr = grbsnav.getElementsByClassName(item);
    var liWidth = liArr[0].offsetWidth;
    var span = grbsnav.getElementsByClassName(spantag)[0];
    // 计数器
    var cnt = 0;

    // for循环绑定事件
    for(var i=0; i<liArr.length; i++){
        // 自定义属性，然后绑定index属性为索引值
        liArr[i].index = i;
        // 鼠标进入事件
        liArr[i].onmouseover = function(){
            // 然span运动到该li的索引值位置
            animate(span, this.index*liWidth);
            cnt = this.index;
            animate(span, cnt*liWidth);
        }
        // 鼠标移开
        liArr[i].onmouseout = function(){
            // span运动到原位置
            animate(span, cnt*liWidth);
        }
    }
}

// 缓动动画封装
function animate(element, target){
    // 清除间歇调用
    clearInterval(element.timer);
    // 设置超时调用
    element.timer = setInterval(function(){
        // 设置步数
        var step = (target - element.offsetLeft)/10;
        // 调整步数
        step = step > 0 ? Math.ceil(step) : Math.floor(step);
        // 设置样式
        element.style.left = element.offsetLeft + step + "px";
        // console.log(1);
        if(Math.abs(target - element.offsetLeft) < Math.abs(step)){
            element.style.left = target + "px";
            clearInterval(element.timer);
        }
    }, 20);
}

}

//去掉特殊字符
function checkName(val){ 
    var reg = new RegExp("[`~!@#$^&*()=|{}':;',\\[\\].<>/?~！@#￥……&*（）——|{}【】‘；：”“'。，、？]"); 
    var rs = ""; 
    for (var i = 0, l = val.length; i < val.length; i++) { 
        rs = rs + val.substr(i, 1).replace(reg, ''); 
    } 
    return rs; 
}

//请求回调打开地址
function newWindow(url, id) { 
	var a = document.createElement('a'); 
	a.setAttribute('href', url); 
	a.setAttribute('target', '_blank');
	a.setAttribute('id', id); 
	if(!document.getElementById(id)) { 
	document.body.appendChild(a);
	} 
	a.click(); 
}

     function loginmmnumget(){
        $yt.ajax.svr({
              url: "e:YiTian.action.LoginAction.getMmDay",
              suc: function (msg) {
                 if(msg.data==-1)
                 {
                    layer.open({
                    	type:2,offset: '10px'
                    	,area: ['500px', '294px']
                    	,title:["温馨提示：免密登录设置","background:#1281c8!important;color:#ffffff;"]
                        ,content:["/eptemp.aspx?t=Znzw.manage.mmloginSet&istest=1","no"]
                        ,cancel: function(index, layero){ 
                        	//点击关闭免密登录设置
                        	$yt.ajax.svr({
					            url: "e:YiTian.action.LoginAction.setMmDay",dbconn:"DbDefault",
					            data:{days:0},
					            suc: function (msg) {
					            	layer.close(index)
					            }
					        });
						  return false; 
						}
                        });
                 }
              }
        });

function xzarea1(xzareacode){
	var oorgCode=getParam('oorgCode');
	var str='';
	var param={
		"areaCode":xzareacode
	}
	$yt.ajax.post("ZWBSDB","e:ZnzwSvr.page.OrgManageAction.GetOrgInfoListCJ",param,function(res){
		if(res.code=="0"){
			if(res.data!=null&&res.data.length>0){
				var data=res.data;
				for(var i=0;i<res.data.length;i++){
					str+='<a onclick="openlink(\'/jdANDcPage.do?ShortCode='+data[i].ShortCode+'&oorgCode='+data[i].OOrgcode+'\')">'+
							'<div class="areaname xzitem" oorgcode="'+data[i].OOrgcode+'" shortcode="'+data[i].ShortCode+'">'+data[i].ShortName+'</div>'+
						  '</a>';
				}
				$('#xzarea').html(str);
				$('.xzitem').each(function(i){
					if($(this).attr('oorgcode')==oorgCode){
						$('#cityname').text($(this).text());
						$('#cityname').attr('code',$(this).attr('shortcode'));
						$('#cityname').attr('title',$(this).text());
						$('.local_webname').text($(this).text());
					}
				});
			}else{
				$('#xzarea').html('');
			}
		}
	},true,"",true);
}
	//问候语
function wenhou($){
		var now = new Date(),hour = now.getHours() 
		if(hour < 6){
			$('.welcome').text("凌晨好！");
			}
		else if (hour < 9){
			$('.welcome').text("早上好！")
		}
		else if (hour < 12){
			$('.welcome').text("上午好！")}
		else if (hour < 14){
			$('.welcome').text("中午好！")}
		else if (hour < 17){
			$('.welcome').text("下午好！")
		}
		/*else if (hour < 19){
			$('.welcome').text("傍晚好！")}*/
		else if (hour < 22){
			$('.welcome').text("晚上好！")
		}
		else {
			$('.welcome').text("夜里好！")
		}
	}

function openlink(url){
	if(url==""){
	  alert("未发现链接地址");
	  return false;
	}
  if(url.indexOf("zwfw.guizhou.gov.cn")!=-1||url.indexOf(".do")!=-1||url.indexOf("eptemp.aspx")!=-1){
		var qycode=getParam("areacode");
		if(qycode==""||qycode==null||qycode=="null"||!qycode){
			qycode="520000";
		}
		if(url.indexOf("?") == -1){
			location.href=url+'?areacode='+qycode;
		}else{
			location.href=url+'&areacode='+qycode;
		}
	}else{
		location.href=url
	}
}	

function Nopenlink(url){
	if(url.indexOf("gov.cn")>0){
		var qycode=getParam("areacode");
		if(qycode==""||qycode==null||qycode=="null"||!qycode){
			qycode="520000";
		}
		if(url.indexOf("?") == -1){
			window.open(url+'?areacode='+qycode);
		}else{
			if(getParam("areacode")!=""){
				window.open(url);
			}else{
				window.open(url+'&areacode='+qycode);
			}
		}
	}else{
		if(confirm("您访问的链接即将离开”贵州省人民政府门户网站“，是否继续？")){
			window.open(url);
		}
	}
}
//乡镇
function xzarea(xzareacode){
	var oorgCode=getParam('oorgCode');
	var str='';
	var param={"areaCode":xzareacode};
	$.get("/xzareadata.do",param,function(res){
		//console.log("乡镇");
		//console.log(res);
		if(res.code=="0"){
				if(res.data!=null&&res.data.length>0){
					var data=res.data;
					for(var i=0;i<res.data.length;i++){
						str+='<li class="" shortcode="'+data[i].ShortCode+'" oorgcode="'+data[i].OOrgcode+'" title="'+data[i].ShortName+'" areacode="'+data[i].AreaCode+'">'+data[i].ShortName+'<span class="layui-btn xzselect" shortcode="'+data[i].ShortCode+'" oorgcode="'+data[i].OOrgcode+'">切换到'+data[i].ShortName+'</span></li>';
					}
					$('#areaFour').html(str);
					$('.shownmb').show();
					var ShortCode=getParam("ShortCode");
					$('#areaFour li').each(function(i){
						if($(this).attr('oorgcode')==oorgCode){
							$('#areaFour li').removeClass('xzact');
							$(this).addClass('xzact')
							$('.xzselect').hide();
							$('.xzselect').eq(i).show();
							$('#cityname').text($(this).attr('title'));
							$('#cityname').attr('code',$(this).attr('shortcode'));
							$('#cityname').attr('title',$(this).attr('title'));
							$('.yzname').text($(this).text());
						}
						if(i==0){
							$('#areaFour li').removeClass('xzact');
							$(this).addClass('xzact')
							$('.xzselect').hide();
							$('.xzselect').eq(i).show();
							cunju($(this).attr('shortcode'),$(this).attr('oorgcode'));
						}
						$(this).click(function(){
							$('#areaFour li').removeClass('xzact');
							$(this).addClass('xzact')
							$('.xzselect').hide();
							$('.xzselect').eq(i).show();
							cunju($(this).attr('shortcode'),$(this).attr('oorgcode'));
						});
					});
					$('.xzselect').each(function(i){
						$(this).click(function(){
							location.href='/eptemp.aspx?t=Znzw.bgt_Html.bgt_ty.bgt_cj&istest=1&ShortCode='+$(this).attr('shortcode')+'&oorgCode='+$(this).attr('oorgcode')+'&bmcode='+$(this).attr('oorgcode')+'&areacode='+$(this).attr('shortcode').substring(0,6);
						});
					});
				}else{
					$('#areaFour').html('');
					$('#areaFive').html('');
					$('.shownmb').hide()
					$('.showxj').hide();
					$('.showxj').eq(0).show();
					$('.titem-nav').removeClass('titem-navact');
					$('.titem-nav').eq(0).addClass('titem-navact');
				}
			}
	},"json")
}

//机构
function areaOrg(obj,areacode,supcode){
	var str='';
	var param={"areaCode":areacode};
	$.get("/bmlist.do",param,function(res){
		 if(res.code=="0"){
				if(res.data!=null&&res.data.length>0){
					var data=res.data;
					for(var i=0;i<res.data.length;i++){
						if(data[i].MbUrl){
							str+='<li><a href="'+data[i].MbUrl+'&ocode='+data[i].OOrgcode+'&orgcode='+data[i].Orgcode+'&areacode='+data[i].AreaCode+'" target="_bank">'+data[i].Orgname+'</a></li>';
						}else{
							str+='<li><a href="/eptemp.aspx?t=Znzw.bgt_Html.bgt_html.bgt_bmqjd&istest=1&ocode='+data[i].OOrgcode+'&areacode='+data[i].AreaCode+'" >'+data[i].Orgname+'</a></li>';
						}
					}
					$('#areaOrg').html(str);
					if(supcode=="520000"){
						$("#areatitle").html($(obj).find('.qname').text()+"（区、县）");
					}
					$("#textOrgName").html($(obj).find('.qname').text()+"部门");
				}else{
					$('#areaOrg').html('');
				}
			}
	},"json");
}
//村居
function cunju(orgAreaCode,oorgCode){
	var str='';
	var param={"orgAreaCode":orgAreaCode,"oorgCode":oorgCode};
	$.get("/cunjudata.do",param,function(res){
		if(res.code=="0"){
				if(res.data!=null&&res.data.length>0){
					var data=res.data;
					for(var i=0;i<res.data.length;i++){
						str+='<li><a href="/eptemp.aspx?t=Znzw.bgt_Html.bgt_ty.bgt_cj&istest=1&ShortCode='+data[i].ShortCode+'&oorgCode='+data[i].OOParentCode+'&bmcode='+data[i].OOrgcode+'&areacode='+data[i].ShortCode+'" shortcode="'+data[i].ShortCode+'" ooparentcode="'+data[i].OOParentCode+'" title="'+data[i].ShortName+'" target="_bank">'+data[i].ShortName+'</a></li>';
					}
					$('#areaFive').html(str);
				}else{
					$('#areaFive').html('');
				}
			}
	},"json");
}

function linkhref(url,obj){
	var areacode=getParam("areacode");
	if(areacode!=null){
		window.location.href=replaceParamVal('areacode',obj);
	}else{
		window.location.href=window.location.href+'?areacode='+obj;
	}
}
//获取常用站点
function getcyArea(){
	var url=window.location.href
	$yt.ajax.post("ZWBSDB","e:ZnzwSvr.page.DictInfoAction.GetCYZD","",function(res){
		if(res.code=="0"){
			if(res.data!=null){//如果常用站点不为空
				if(url.indexOf("?") == -1){
					window.location.href=window.location.href+"?areacode="+res.data.code;
				}else{
					window.location.href=window.location.href+"&areacode="+res.data.code;
				}
			}else{
			}
		}
	},true,"",true);
}
//重置登录状态
function loginInfo(){
	$yt.ajax.post("","e:YiTian.action.LoginAction.Get","",function(res){
    if(res.code=="0"){
     	if(res.data!=null){
     		 $("#userid").val(res.data.UserID);
	     	 if(res.data.TBind!=null){
		     	 $("#tel").val(res.data.TBind.MOBILE);
		     	 $("#utype").val(res.data.TBind.USER_TYPE);
	     	 }
	       	 localStorage.setItem("islogin","True");
       	}else{
	       	 localStorage.setItem("islogin","False");
	     }
    }
   },true,"",true);
}

								                  	  	$('.grzzul').eq(i).show();

								                  	  	$('.zzlist').eq(i).show();

								                  //获取证照数据
								                  function getZZList($,layer,ctype,areacode){
														if(ctype==1){
															var str='',str1='',str2='',listr='';
															var param={
																"areaCode":areacode,
																"ctype":ctype,
																"isrd":1
															}
															$yt.ajax.post("ZWBSDB","e:ZnzwSvr.page.ManageAction.GetZZServiceInfo",param,function(res){
																	//console.log("获取证照数据")
																	//console.log(res)
																	if(res.code=="0"){
																		if(res.data!=null&&res.data.length>0){
																			var data=res.data;
																			for(var i=0;i<data.length;i++){
																				if(i<6){
																					str+='<div class="layui-col-xs4">'+
																							'<div class="zzitem grzzitem" style="padding:10px;" mid="'+data[i].mid+'" ctype="'+data[i].ctype+'" outitemCode="'+data[i].outitemCode+'" title="'+data[i].name+'">'+
																								'<img src="source/znzw/icon/zzicom.png" style="width:100%;">'+
																								'<p class="layui-elip">'+data[i].name+'</p>'+
																							'</div>'+
																						'</div>';
																					if(i==0){
																						listr+='<li></li>';
																					}
																				}
																				if(i>5&&i<12){
																					str1+='<div class="layui-col-xs4">'+
																							'<div class="zzitem grzzitem" style="padding:10px;" mid="'+data[i].mid+'" ctype="'+data[i].ctype+'" outitemCode="'+data[i].outitemCode+'" title="'+data[i].name+'">'+
																								'<img src="source/znzw/icon/zzicom.png" style="width:100%;">'+
																								'<p class="layui-elip">'+data[i].name+'</p>'+
																							'</div>'+
																						'</div>';
																					if(i==6){
																						listr+='<li></li>';
																					}

																					str2+='<div class="layui-col-xs4">'+
																							'<div class="zzitem grzzitem" style="padding:10px;" mid="'+data[i].mid+'" ctype="'+data[i].ctype+'" outitemCode="'+data[i].outitemCode+'" title="'+data[i].name+'">'+

			<script>
			var areacode=getParam("areacode");
			/*获取部门列表数据*/
			function getbmlist($,form,areacode){
				var str='';
				var param={
					"areaCode":areacode
				}
				//console.log(param);
				$.get("/bmlist.do",param,function(res){
				//$yt.ajax.post("","e:ZnzwSvr.page.OrgManageAction.GetOrgInfoList",param,function(res){//bmlist.do
					//console.log("获取部门数据列表");
					//console.log(res);
					if(res.code=="0"){
						if(res.data){
							var data=res.data;
							//console.log(data);
							if(data.length>0){
								for(var i=0;i<data.length;i++){
								 	str+='<div  class="layui-col-xs3 lch_list-item bmfont" mburl="'+data[i].MbUrl+'" ocode="'+data[i].OOrgcode+'" orgcode="'+data[i].Orgcode+'" title="'+data[i].Orgname+'">'+data[i].Orgname+'</div>';
								}
								$('#bmlistdata').html(str);
								//截取部门名称
								$('.bmfont').each(function(i){
									var text=$(this).text().substring(0,3);
									var bmname=$(this).text();
									if (text.indexOf('贵州') !=-1) {
									    $(this).text(bmname.substring(2,bmname.length));
									 }
								});
								var arr=[];
								if(arr.length==0){
									$('.into_btn').unbind("click").click(function(){
								  	/*if($(this).attr('mburl')){
								  		openlink($(this).attr('mburl')+'&ocode='+$(this).attr('ocode')+'&orgcode='+$(this).attr('orgcode')+'&areacode='+areacode);
								  	}else{*/
								  		openlink('/eptemp.aspx?t=Znzw.bgt_Html.bgt_html.bgt_bmqjd&istest=1&ocode='+$(this).attr('ocode')+'&orgcode='+$(this).attr('orgcode'));
								  	//}
								  	var hotparam={
										"code":$(this).attr("ocode"),//事项编码，部门编码，便民服务便编码
										"areacode":areacode,//区域code
										"name":$(this).attr("title"),//名称
										"hotnum":1,//数量
										"flag":"deprt",//item,事项;deprt,部门;bmser,便民服务
										"url":"",//地址
										"ico":"",//图标
									}
									saveHitNum($,hotparam);//保存点击数
								  });
								}
								$('.lch_list-item').each(function(i){
									$(this).click(function(e){
										////console.log(55555555555555555)
										e.stopPropagation();
										if($('.lch_tips').is(':visible')){
						                	$('.lch_tips').slideToggle();
						                }
										$('.into_btn').attr('ocode',$(this).attr('ocode'));
										$('.into_btn').attr('title',$(this).attr('title'));
										$('.into_btn').attr('orgcode',$(this).attr('orgcode'));
						           		$('.into_btn').attr('mburl',$(this).attr('mburl'));
										var navstr='';
										var ocode=$(this).attr('ocode');
										$('.lch_tips').slideUp();
										$('.bmdown').html('<i class="layui-icon layui-icon-down"></i');
										$('#gengduo').attr('ocode',$(this).attr('ocode'));
							            $('#gengduo').attr('orgcode',$(this).attr('orgcode'));
										getBMSXLsit($,areacode,$(this).attr('ocode'),"");
										BMfwapply($,$(this).attr('ocode'),$(this).attr('orgcode'));
										if(i==0){
											arr=data.slice(i,i+6);
										}else if(i==1){
											arr=data.slice(i-1,i+5);
										}else if(i==2){
											arr=data.slice(i-2,i+4);
										}else if(i==3){
											arr=data.slice(i-3,i+3);
										}else{
											if(i>3&&i<=data.length-3){
											   arr=data.slice(i-3,i+3);
											}else if(i==data.length-2){
												arr=data.slice(i-4,i+2);
											}else if(i==data.length-1){
												arr=data.slice(i-5,i+1);
											}
										}
										//console.log(arr);
										if(arr.length>0){
											for(var k=0;k<arr.length;k++){
												navstr+='<div class="layui-elip lch_bm_nav_item bmfont" mburl="'+arr[k].MbUrl+'" ocode="'+arr[k].OOrgcode+'" orgcode="'+arr[k].Orgcode+'" title="'+arr[k].Orgname+'">'+arr[k].Orgname+'</div>';
											}
											$('#bmnavlist').html(navstr);
											//截取部门名称
											$('.bmfont').each(function(i){
												var text=$(this).text().substring(0,3);
												var bmname=$(this).text();
												if (text.indexOf('贵州') !=-1) {
												    $(this).text(bmname.substring(2,bmname.length));
												  }
											});
										  $('.into_btn').unbind("click").click(function(){
										  //console.log(44444444444444444)
										  	/*if($(this).attr('mburl')){
										  		openlink($(this).attr('mburl')+'&ocode='+$(this).attr('ocode')+'&orgcode='+$(this).attr('orgcode')+'&areacode='+areacode);
										  	}else{*/
										  		openlink('/eptemp.aspx?t=Znzw.bgt_Html.bgt_html.bgt_bmqjd&istest=1&ocode='+$(this).attr('ocode')+'&orgcode='+$(this).attr('orgcode')+'&areacode='+areacode);
										  	//}
										  	var hotparam={
												"code":$(this).attr("ocode"),//事项编码，部门编码，便民服务便编码
												"areacode":areacode,//区域code
												"name":$(this).attr("title"),//名称
												"hotnum":1,//数量
												"flag":"deprt",//item,事项;deprt,部门;bmser,便民服务
												"url":"",//地址
												"ico":"",//图标
											}
											saveHitNum($,hotparam);//保存点击数
											form.render('select');
										  });
											$('.lch_bm_nav_item').each(function(j){
									           if(ocode==$(this).attr('ocode')){
									           		$('.into_btn').attr('ocode',$(this).attr('ocode'));
													$('.into_btn').attr('title',$(this).attr('title'));
													$('.into_btn').attr('orgcode',$(this).attr('orgcode'));
									           		$('.into_btn').attr('mburl',$(this).attr('mburl'));
									           		$("#select").attr("ocode",$(this).attr('ocode'));
									           		$("#homeSreach").attr("ocode",$(this).attr('ocode'));
									           		$('#gengduo').attr('ocode',$(this).attr('ocode'));
									                $('#gengduo').attr('orgcode',$(this).attr('orgcode'));
									                $('.lch_bm_nav_item').removeClass('lch_bm_nav_item_active');
									                $(this).addClass('lch_bm_nav_item_active');
									           		getBMSXLsit($,areacode,$(this).attr('ocode'),"");
									           		BMfwapply($,$(this).attr('ocode'),$(this).attr('orgcode'))
									           }
									           $(this).click(function(e){
									           		////console.log(3333333333333333333)
									           		e.stopPropagation();
									           		if($('.lch_tips').is(':visible')){
									                	$('.lch_tips').slideToggle();
									                }
									           		$('.into_btn').attr('ocode',$(this).attr('ocode'));
													$('.into_btn').attr('title',$(this).attr('title'));
													$('.into_btn').attr('orgcode',$(this).attr('orgcode'));
									           		$('.into_btn').attr('mburl',$(this).attr('mburl'));
									           		$("#select").attr("ocode",$(this).attr('ocode'));
									           		$("#homeSreach").attr("ocode",$(this).attr('ocode'));
									               	$('.lch_bm_nav_item').removeClass('lch_bm_nav_item_active');
									                $(this).addClass('lch_bm_nav_item_active');
									                $('#gengduo').attr('ocode',$(this).attr('ocode'));
									                $('#gengduo').attr('orgcode',$(this).attr('orgcode'));
									                getBMSXLsit($,areacode,$(this).attr('ocode'),"");
									                BMfwapply($,$(this).attr('ocode'),$(this).attr('orgcode'))
									                form.render('select');
									           });
									        });
										}
									});
								});
							}else{
								$('#bmlistdata').html('<div style="padding:10px;">暂无数据</div>');
							}
						}else{
								$('#bmlistdata').html('<div style="padding:10px;">暂无数据</div>');
							}
					}else{
						$('#bmlistdata').html('<div style="padding:10px;">'+res.data+'</div>');
					}
				},"json");
			}

							<script>
								$(function(){
									homesxlist();
								});
								function homesxlist(){
									var qycode=getParam("areacode");
									var param={"areacode":qycode?qycode:"520000"}
									$.get("/eptemp.aspx?t=Znzw.bgt_Html.bgt_ty.bgt_homesxlist&istest=1",param,function(data){
										  //console.log("param:-----------"+param)
										  ////console.log(data);
										if(data){
											 $('#homesxlist').empty();
             								 $('#homesxlist').html(data);
             								 $('.lch_bm_nav_item').each(function(i){
										       if(i==0){
										       		$('.into_btn').attr('ocode',$(this).attr('ocode'));
													$('.into_btn').attr('title',$(this).attr('title'));
													$('.into_btn').attr('orgcode',$(this).attr('orgcode'));
										       		$('.into_btn').attr('mburl',$(this).attr('mburl'));
										       		$("#select").attr("ocode",$(this).attr('ocode'));
										       		$("#homeSreach").attr("ocode",$(this).attr('ocode'));
										       		$('#gengduo').attr('ocode',$(this).attr('ocode'));
										            $('#gengduo').attr('orgcode',$(this).attr('orgcode'));
										       		getBMSXLsit($,qycode,$(this).attr('ocode'),"");
										       		BMfwapply($,$(this).attr('ocode'),$(this).attr('orgcode'))
										       }
										       $(this).click(function(e){
										       //console.log(1111111111111)
										       		e.stopPropagation();
										       		$('.into_btn').attr('ocode',$(this).attr('ocode'));
													$('.into_btn').attr('title',$(this).attr('title'));
													$('.into_btn').attr('orgcode',$(this).attr('orgcode'));
										       		$('.into_btn').attr('mburl',$(this).attr('mburl'));
										       		$("#select").attr("ocode",$(this).attr('ocode'));
										       		$("#homeSreach").attr("ocode",$(this).attr('ocode'));
										           	$('.lch_bm_nav_item').removeClass('lch_bm_nav_item_active');
										            $(this).addClass('lch_bm_nav_item_active');
										            $('#gengduo').attr('ocode',$(this).attr('ocode'));
										            $('#gengduo').attr('orgcode',$(this).attr('orgcode'));
										            getBMSXLsit($,qycode,$(this).attr('ocode'),"");
										            BMfwapply($,$(this).attr('ocode'),$(this).attr('orgcode'))
										            if($('.lch_tips').is(':visible')){
										            	$('.lch_tips').slideToggle();
										            }
										       });
										  	});
											$('.bmdown').click(function(e){
											//console.log(222222222222222222)
												e.stopPropagation();
												if($('.lch_tips').is(':hidden')){
													$('.bmdown').html('<i class="layui-icon layui-icon-up"></i');
												}else{
													$('.bmdown').html('<i class="layui-icon layui-icon-down"></i');
												}
												$('.lch_tips').slideToggle();
											});
											//截取部门名称
											$('.bmfont').each(function(i){
												var text=$(this).text().substring(0,3);
												var bmname=$(this).text();
												if (text.indexOf('贵州') !=-1) {
												    $(this).text(bmname.substring(2,bmname.length));
												  }
											});
										}

								        var widths=$('.grfenlei').outerWidth();
								        $('.grfenlei').find('.rd-fenlei').each(function(i){
								        	if(i%4==0){
								        		count=0
								        	}else{
								        		count++
								        	}
								        	var left=155*count+0.38*count;
								        	//console.log(left)
								        	$('.grfenlei').find('.re-hover').eq(i).css({'margin-left':-left});
								        });
								        $('.grfenlei').find('.re-hover').each(function(i){
								        	$(this).hover(function(){
								        		//console.log(i)
								        		$('.grfenlei').find('.rd-fenlei').eq(i).addClass('rdact');
								        	},function(){
								        		$('.grfenlei').find('.rd-fenlei').eq(i).removeClass('rdact');

									$(function(){
										var count=0;
								        var widths=$('.frfenlei').outerWidth();
								        $('.frfenlei').find('.rd-fenlei').each(function(i){
								        	if(i%4==0){
								        		count=0
								        	}else{
								        		count++
								        	}
								        	var left=155*count+0.38*count;
								        	//console.log(left)
								        	$('.frfenlei').find('.re-hover').eq(i).css({'margin-left':-left});
								        });
								        $('.frfenlei').find('.re-hover').each(function(i){
								        	$(this).hover(function(){
								        		//console.log(i)
								        		$('.frfenlei').find('.rd-fenlei').eq(i).addClass('rdact');
								        	},function(){
								        		$('.frfenlei').find('.rd-fenlei').eq(i).removeClass('rdact');
								        	});
								        });
									});

//获取用户登录信息保存用户足迹
var saveparam={
	"userid":"",//用户id
	"title":"",//标题
	"keyword":"",//关键词
	"fwurl":"",//页面地址
	"itemcode":"",//事项编码
	"itemname":"",//事项名称
	"itemtype":"",//事项类型
	"typename":"",//类型名称
	"areacode":""//区域编码
}

function getUserInfo($,param){
	$yt.ajax.post("","e:YiTian.action.LoginAction.Get","",function(res){
         		console.log("获取用户登录信息保存用户足迹");
		 		console.log(res);
 		if(res.code=="0"){
 			if(res.data!=null){
 				if(res.data.UserID>0){
 					param.userid=res.data.UserID;
 					saveUserZj($,param);
 				}else{
 					param.userid='';
 					saveUserZj($,param);
 				}
 			}else{
 				param.userid='';
 				saveUserZj($,param);
 			}
 		}else{
 			param.userid='';
 			saveUserZj($,param);
 		}
 	},true,"",true);
}

//保存用户足迹
function saveUserZj($,param){
	/*zinfo//json实体//
	*
	*userid//用户id
	*title//标题
	*keyword//关键词
	*fwurl//页面地址
	*itemcode//事项编码
	*itemname//事项名称
	*itemtype//事项类型
	*typename//类型名称
	*areacode//区域编码
	*
	*/
	console.log(param);
	saveparam.userid=param.userid;
	saveparam.title=param.title.replace(/\s*/g,"");
	saveparam.keyword=param.keyword;
	saveparam.fwurl=param.fwurl;
	saveparam.itemcode=param.itemcode;
	saveparam.itemname=param.itemname.replace(/\s*/g,"");
	saveparam.itemtype=param.itemtype;
	saveparam.typename=param.typename.replace(/\s*/g,"");
	saveparam.areacode=param.areacode;
	$yt.ajax.post("ZWBSDB","e:ZnzwSvr.action.UserZJAction.SaveUserZJ",saveparam,function(res){
		console.log('保存用户足迹');
		console.log(param);
		console.log(res);
		if(res.code=="0"){
			if(res.data==true){
				console.log('保存成功');
			}
		}
	},true,"",true);
}
/** 
 * 获取指定的URL参数值 
 * URL:http://www.quwan.com/index?name=tyler 
 * 参数：paramName URL参数 
 * 调用方法:getParam("name") 
 * 返回值:tyler 
 */ 
function getParam(paramName) {
    paramValue = "", isFound = !1; 
    if (this.location.search.indexOf("?") == 0 && this.location.search.indexOf("=") > 1) { 
        arrSource = decodeURI(this.location.search).substring(1, this.location.search.length).split("&"), i = 0; 
        while (i < arrSource.length && !isFound) arrSource[i].indexOf("=") > 0 && arrSource[i].split("=")[0].toLowerCase() == paramName.toLowerCase() && (paramValue = arrSource[i].split("=")[1], isFound = !0), i++ 
    } 
    if(paramValue==null || paramValue==""){
       return paramValue  == "" && (paramValue  = null), paramValue
    }else{
       return removeXss(paramValue);
    }
    //return paramValue  == "" && (paramValue  = null), paramValue?removeXss(paramValue):null
}

function removeXss(val)
    {
        val = val.replace(/([\x00-\x08][\x0b-\x0c][\x0e-\x20])/g, '');

        var search = 'abcdefghijklmnopqrstuvwxyz';
        search += 'ABCDEFGHIJKLMNOPQRSTUVWXYZ';
        search += '1234567890!@#$%^&*()';
        search += '~`";:?+/={}[]-_|\'\\';

        for (var i = 0; i < search.length; i++) {
            var re = new RegExp('(&#[x|X]0{0,8}'+ parseInt(search[i].charCodeAt(),16)+';?)','gi');
            val = val.replace(re, search[i]);
            re = new RegExp('(&#0{0,8}'+ search[i].charCodeAt() + ';?)','gi');
            val = val.replace(re, search[i]);
        }

        var ra1 = ['javascript', 'vbscript', 'expression', 'applet', 'meta','blink', 'link',  'script', 'embed', 'object', 'iframe', 'frame', 'frameset', 'ilayer', 'layer', 'bgsound', 'title'];
        var ra2 = ['onabort', 'onactivate', 'onafterprint', 'onafterupdate', 'onbeforeactivate', 'onbeforecopy', 'onbeforecut', 'onbeforedeactivate', 'onbeforeeditfocus', 'onbeforepaste', 'onbeforeprint', 'onbeforeunload', 'onbeforeupdate', 'onblur', 'onbounce', 'oncellchange', 'onchange', 'onclick', 'oncontextmenu', 'oncontrolselect', 'oncopy', 'oncut', 'ondataavailable', 'ondatasetchanged', 'ondatasetcomplete', 'ondblclick', 'ondeactivate', 'ondrag', 'ondragend', 'ondragenter', 'ondragleave', 'ondragover', 'ondragstart', 'ondrop', 'onerror', 'onerrorupdate', 'onfilterchange', 'onfinish', 'onfocus', 'onfocusin', 'onfocusout', 'onhelp', 'onkeydown', 'onkeypress', 'onkeyup', 'onlayoutcomplete', 'onload', 'onlosecapture', 'onmousedown', 'onmouseenter', 'onmouseleave', 'onmousemove', 'onmouseout', 'onmouseover', 'onmouseup', 'onmousewheel', 'onmove', 'onmoveend', 'onmovestart', 'onpaste', 'onpropertychange', 'onreadystatechange', 'onreset', 'onresize', 'onresizeend', 'onresizestart', 'onrowenter', 'onrowexit', 'onrowsdelete', 'onrowsinserted', 'onscroll', 'onselect', 'onselectionchange', 'onselectstart', 'onstart', 'onstop', 'onsubmit', 'onunload'];
        var ra = [].concat(ra1, ra2);

        var found = true;
        while (found == true) {
            var val_before = val;
            for (var i = 0; i < ra.length; i++) {
                var pattern = '';
                for (var j = 0; j < ra[i].length; j++) {
                    if (j > 0) {
                        pattern += '(';
                        pattern += '(&#[x|X]0{0,8}([9][a][b]);?)?';
                        pattern += '|(&#0{0,8}([9][10][13]);?)?';
                        pattern += ')?';
                    }
                    pattern += ra[i][j];
                }
                parttern = new RegExp(pattern,'gi');
                var replacement = ra[i].substr(0, 2) + '<x>'+ ra[i].substr(2);
                val = val.replace(parttern, replacement);
                if (val_before  == val) {
                    found = false;
                }
            }
        }
        return val;
  }

function replaceParamVal(paramName,replaceWith) {
    var oUrl = this.location.href.toString();
    var re=eval('/('+ paramName+'=)([^&]*)/gi');
    var nUrl = oUrl.replace(re,paramName+'='+replaceWith);
    console.log(nUrl);
    return nUrl;
}

//修改地址参数
function changeURLArg(url,arg,arg_val){ 
   var pattern=arg+'=([^&]*)'; 
   var replaceText=arg+'='+arg_val; 
   if(url.match(pattern)){ 
       var tmp='/('+ arg+'=)([^&]*)/gi'; 
       tmp=url.replace(eval(tmp),replaceText); 
       return tmp; 
   }else{ 
       if(url.match('[\?]')){ 
           return url+'&'+replaceText; 
       }else{ 
           return url+'?'+replaceText; 
       } 
  } 
   return url+'\n'+arg+'\n'+arg_val; 
}

	  type: 2,
	  title:title?title:false,

	  area: ['60%', '80%'],
	  closeBtn:2,
	  scrollbar:false,
	  move:false,
	  content: url //iframe的url
	});
}

//获取智能消息提醒
function znMsg($,atag,content,islogin){
	if(content){
		var i=0;
		var timer;
		if(islogin == true){
			$(".txbox").show();
			$(".txbox").addClass('layui-anim-scale');
			timer = setInterval(function(){
		        $('.wz-div').text(content.substring(0, i));
		        i++;
		        if( $('.wz-div').text()==content){
		            clearInterval(timer);
		        };
		    },200);
		    $yt.play.tts(content,"https://zwfw.guizhou.gov.cn");
		}else if(islogin == false){
			timer = setInterval(function(){
		        $('.ts').text(content.substring(0, i));
		        i++;
		        if( $('.ts').text()==content){
		            clearInterval(timer);
		        };
		    },200);
		    $yt.play.tts(content,"https://zwfw.guizhou.gov.cn");
		}
	}else{
		$yt.ajax.post("","e:ZnzwSvr.action.AlertAction.getAlert",{"atag":atag},function(res){
			console.log("获取智能消息提醒");
		   console.log(res)
		   if(res.code=="0"){
		   	var data=res.data
		   	if(data){
		   		if(data.acontent){
			   		$(".txbox").show();
			   		$(".txbox").addClass('layui-anim-scale');
				   //$yt.play.tts("您好，欢迎来到淘政务主题服务馆，我是客服小姐姐，贵宝","http://103.3.152.215:84");
				   var str=data.acontent;
				   var i=0;
				   var timer = setInterval(function(){
				        $('.wz-div').text(str.substring(0, i));
				        $('.ts').text(str.substring(0, i));
				        i++;
				        if($('.wz-div').text()==str){
				            clearInterval(timer);
				        };
				         if( $('.ts').text()==str){
				            clearInterval(timer);
				        };
				    },200);
			   		$yt.play.tts(data.acontent,"https://zwfw.guizhou.gov.cn");
			   	}
		   	}
		   	var t = setInterval(function(){
				$(".txbox").hide();
				$(".txbox").removeClass('layui-anim-scale');
				 clearInterval(t);
			}, 15000);
		   }
		  },true,"",true);
	  }
}
function navhd(grbsnav,item,spantag){
	// 鼠标放在哪个li上面，span对应一道到哪里，移开后回到原位置
    var grbsnav=document.getElementById(grbsnav);
    var liArr = grbsnav.getElementsByClassName(item);
    var liWidth = liArr[0].offsetWidth;
    var span = grbsnav.getElementsByClassName(spantag)[0];
    // 计数器
    var cnt = 0;

    // for循环绑定事件
    for(var i=0; i<liArr.length; i++){
        // 自定义属性，然后绑定index属性为索引值
        liArr[i].index = i;
        // 鼠标进入事件
        liArr[i].onmouseover = function(){
            // 然span运动到该li的索引值位置
            animate(span, this.index*liWidth);
            cnt = this.index;
            animate(span, cnt*liWidth);
        }
        // 鼠标移开
        liArr[i].onmouseout = function(){
            // span运动到原位置
            animate(span, cnt*liWidth);
        }
    }
}

// 缓动动画封装
function animate(element, target){
    // 清除间歇调用
    clearInterval(element.timer);
    // 设置超时调用
    element.timer = setInterval(function(){
        // 设置步数
        var step = (target - element.offsetLeft)/10;
        // 调整步数
        step = step > 0 ? Math.ceil(step) : Math.floor(step);
        // 设置样式
        element.style.left = element.offsetLeft + step + "px";
        // console.log(1);
        if(Math.abs(target - element.offsetLeft) < Math.abs(step)){
            element.style.left = target + "px";
            clearInterval(element.timer);
        }
    }, 20);
}

//去掉特殊字符
function checkName(val){ 
    var reg = new RegExp("[`~!@#$^&*()=|{}':;',\\[\\].<>/?~！@#￥……&*（）——|{}【】‘；：”“'。，、？]"); 
    var rs = ""; 
    for (var i = 0, l = val.length; i < val.length; i++) { 
        rs = rs + val.substr(i, 1).replace(reg, ''); 
    } 
    return rs; 
}

//请求回调打开地址
function newWindow(url, id) { 
	var a = document.createElement('a'); 
	a.setAttribute('href', url); 
	a.setAttribute('target', '_blank');
	a.setAttribute('id', id); 
	if(!document.getElementById(id)) { 
	document.body.appendChild(a);
	} 
	a.click(); 
}

// JavaScript Document
(function($){
	$.fn.myScroll = function(options){
	//默认配置
	var defaults = {
		speed:40,  //滚动速度,值越大速度越慢
		rowHeight:24 //每行的高度
	};
	var opts = $.extend({}, defaults, options),intId = [];
	function marquee(obj, step){
		obj.find("ul").animate({
			marginTop: '-=1'
		},0,function(){
				var s = Math.abs(parseInt($(this).css("margin-top")));
				if(s >= step){
					$(this).find("li").slice(0, 1).appendTo($(this));
					$(this).css("margin-top", 0);
				}
			});
		}
		this.each(function(i){
			var sh = opts["rowHeight"],speed = opts["speed"],_this = $(this);
			intId[i] = setInterval(function(){
				if(_this.find("ul").height()<=_this.height()){
					clearInterval(intId[i]);
				}else{
					marquee(_this, sh);
				}
			}, speed);
			_this.hover(function(){
				clearInterval(intId[i]);
			},function(){
				intId[i] = setInterval(function(){
					if(_this.find("ul").height()<=_this.height()){
						clearInterval(intId[i]);
					}else{
						marquee(_this, sh);
					}
				}, speed);
			});
		});
	}
})(jQuery);
(function ($) {
    var timers = [];

    function nextMove(obj, step) {
        obj.find("ul").animate({
            marginLeft: -step
        }, 300, 'swing', function () {
            $(this).find("li").slice(0, 1).appendTo($(this));
            $(this).css("margin-left", 0);
        });
    }

    function preMove(obj, step) {
        var ul = obj.find("ul");
        ul.css('margin-left', -step);
        ul.find("li").last().prependTo(ul);
        ul.animate({
            marginLeft: 0
        }, 300, 'swing', function () {
            ul.css("margin-left", 0);
        });
    }

    function downMove(obj, step) {
        obj.find("ul").animate({
            marginTop: -step
        }, 300, 'swing', function () {
            $(this).find("li").slice(0, 1).appendTo($(this));
            $(this).css("margin-top", 0);
        });
    }

    function upMove(obj, step) {
        var ul = obj.find("ul");
        ul.find("li").last().prependTo(ul);
        ul.css('margin-top', -step);
        ul.animate({
            marginTop: 0
        }, 300, 'swing', function () {
            ul.css("margin-top", 0);
        });
    }

    var methods = {
        init: function (options) {
            var defaults = {
                speed: 3000,//默认时间间隔3s
                direction: 'horizantal'//默认方向水平
            };
            var opts = $.extend({}, defaults, options);

            return this.each(function (i) {
                var speed = opts["speed"] < 1000 ? 3000 : opts["speed"];
                var direction = opts["direction"] == 'vertical' || opts["direction"] == 'horizantal' ? opts["direction"] : 'vertical';
                var _this = $(this);
                var ul = _this.find("ul"), pre = _this.find(".pre"), next = _this.find(".next");
                var sh, isMove, ishori, move, lmove, rmove;
                if (direction == 'horizantal') {
                    isMove = _this.width() < ul.width();
                    ishori = true;
                    move = nextMove;
                    lmove = preMove;
                    rmove = nextMove;
                    sh = ul.find("li:first").outerWidth(true);
                } else {
                    isMove = _this.height() < ul.height();
                    ishori = false;
                    move = downMove;
                    lmove = upMove;
                    rmove = downMove;
                    sh = ul.find("li:first").outerHeight(true);
                }
                if (isMove) {
                    timers[i] = setInterval(function () {
                        move(_this, sh);
                    }, speed);

                    _this.hover(function () {
                        clearInterval(timers[i]);
                    }, function () {
                        timers[i] = setInterval(function () {
                            move(_this, sh);
                        }, speed);
                    });
                    pre.click(function () {
                        lmove(_this, sh);
                    });
                    next.click(function () {
                        rmove(_this, sh);
                    });
                }
            });
        },
        destroy: function () {
            return this.each(function (i) {
                _this = $(this);
                clearInterval(timers[i]);
                _this.find('ul').css({ 'margin-top': 0 });
                _this.find('ul').css({ 'margin-left': 0 });
                _this.unbind("mouseenter").unbind("mouseleave");
                _this.find('.pre').unbind('click');
                _this.find('.next').unbind('click');
            });
        }
    }
    $.fn.mySingleScroll = function (options) {
        var method = arguments[0];
        if (methods[method]) {
            method = methods[method];
        } else if (typeof method == 'object' || !method) {
            method = methods.init;
        } else {
            $.error('error');
            return this;
        }
        return method.apply(this, arguments);
    }
})(jQuery)
var areacode=getParam("areacode");
var t=null;
layui.use(['layer','jquery','carousel','form','element'],function(){
            var layer=layui.layer,
                $=layui.jquery,
                carousel=layui.carousel,
                form=layui.form,
                element=layui.element;

//问候语
function wenhou($){
		var now = new Date(),hour = now.getHours() 
		if(hour < 6){$('.wenhou').text("凌晨好，");}
		else if (hour < 9){$('.wenhou').text("早上好，")}
		else if (hour < 12){$('.wenhou').text("上午好，")}
		else if (hour < 14){$('.wenhou').text("中午好，")}
		else if (hour < 17){$('.wenhou').text("下午好，")}
		//else if (hour < 19){$('.wenhou').text("傍晚好，")}
		else if (hour < 22){$('.wenhou').text("晚上好，")}
		else {$('.wenhou').text("夜里好，")}
}

//链接跳转
function link(url){
	if(areacode!="null"&&areacode&&areacode!=null){
		window.location.href=url+'&areacode='+areacode;
	}else{
		window.location.href=url+'&areacode=520000';
	}
}
//保存点击量
function saveHitNum($,hotparam){
	$yt.ajax.post("ZWBSDB","e:ZnzwSvr.action.HotAction.SaveHotNum",hotparam,function(res){
	},true,"",true);
}

function getlbitem($,layer,flowid,code){
	var Lindex = layer.load();
	$.ajax({ 
       type: "post", 
       url: "/ytbase/system/default.aspx", 
       data:{
       	"yt_out_lay":"1",
       	"DB_Conn":"VISDB",
       	"ClassName":"EPro.API.ApiAction.call",
       	"jkname":"ChainInfo.getChainInfo",
		"regionCode":code,
		"flowId":flowid
       },
       async:false,
       success: function(res){
       		layer.close(Lindex);
       		if(res.code=="0"){
				if(res.data!=null){
					if(res.data.code==200){
						if(res.data.data!=null&&res.data.data.length>0){
							parent.layer.closeAll();
					 		 openlink("/eptemp.aspx?t=Znzw.bgt_Html.bgt_ty.bgt_yjslb_cont&istest=1&areaid="+code+"&flowid="+flowid)
						}else{
							layer.alert('暂未开通', {
							    skin: 'layui-layer-lan'
							    ,title:'温馨提示'
							    ,closeBtn: 1
							    ,time:5000
							    ,anim: 0 //动画类型
							  });
						}
					}else{
						layer.alert('暂未开通', {
						    skin: 'layui-layer-lan' 
						    ,title:'温馨提示'
						    ,closeBtn: 1
						    ,time:5000
						    ,anim: 0 //动画类型
						  });
					}
				}else{
					layer.alert('暂未开通', {
					    skin: 'layui-layer-lan'
					    ,title:'温馨提示'
					    ,closeBtn: 1
					    ,time:5000
					    ,anim: 0 //动画类型
					  });
				}
			}
         },
         error:function(){
         	layer.close(Lindex);
         }
	});
}

//获取好差评统计数据
function getHCPdata(){
	var param={
		"DB_Conn":"VISDB",
		"areacode":""
	};
	//Math.round((n /10000) * 100) / 100;
	$.get("/ytbase/system/?yt_out_lay=1&ClassName=EPro.API.ApiAction.call&jkname=HcpApi.AreaInfo",param,function(res){
		if(res.code=="0"){
			if(res.data!=null){
				$('.dzcount').text(res.data.dzcount);
				$('.lycount').text(res.data.lycount);
				$('.bzcount').text(res.data.bzcount);
				$('.bmycount').text(res.data.bmycount);
				$('.fcbmycount').text(res.data.fcbmycount);
			}
		}
	});
}
//页面公告弹窗
function getWindowPage($,layer){
	var str='';
	$("#ggwindow").html('');
	$.get("/eptemp.aspx?t=Znzw.include.windowPage&istest=1","",function(data){
		if(data){
			str+='<div id="windowPage" style="display:none;">';
			str+=data
			str+='</div>'
			$("#ggwindow").html(str);
			 //页面弹窗
       		layer.open({
			  type: 1,
			  area: ['380px', 'auto'],
			  offset: 'lb',
			  shade: false,
			  title: false, //不显示标题
			  content: $('#windowPage'), //捕获的元素，注意：最好该指定的元素要存放在body最外层，否则可能被其它的相对元素所影响
			  cancel: function(){
			  	$('#windowPage').hide();
			    //关闭操作
			  }
			});
		}
	});
}
//页面漂浮窗口
function moveWindow($,layer){
	var str='';
	$("#floadADwindow").html('');
	var areacode=getParam("areacode");
	var param={"AreaCode":areacode?areacode:"520000"}
	$.get("/eptemp.aspx?t=Znzw.include.moveWindow&istest=1",param,function(data){
		if(data){
			$("#floadADwindow").html(data);
		}
	});
}
